---

## Pattern Legend

| Pattern | Meaning | Action |
|---------|---------|--------|
| DUPLICATE | Exact same data | Keep first, skip second |
| CORRECTION | Same days, different hours | Keep SECOND (the correction) |
| SPLIT | Different days | Need to MERGE both |
